Totalnumberofsistershipstillonorder: ........................................Nil ARCTICVOYAGERfollowsthedesignoftheKawasaki-builtLNGtankerEnergyAdvance (SignificantShipsof2005) veryclosely, butwiththeimportantadditionofeaturesenablinghertoperatesuccessfullyintheharshArcticenvironmentsurroundingthemergingNorwegianSnøhvitLNGproductionproject. Despiteitsimilaritytothearliership, thedesignofthesenewvesselshasbeenpreparedbyMitsuiEngineering & Shipbuilding, andthatcompanyhasalsodeliveredthefirstvesseltoenterservice, drawingheavilyontheaccumulatedexperienceofDetNorskeVeritasrelatingtothestructuralandhumanproblemsofoperatinginArcticonditions.
ArcticVoyageristhe16thKawasaki-builtLNGtankertousetheMossphericalcargotankcontainmentsystem, andisfittedwithfourindependentanksofidenticalsize, holdingatotalof142,700m3atafillingratiof98.5% andtemperatureof -163oC. Liketheship'smainhullstructure, thetanks, andtankskirtwhichsupportsthem, satisfythe25-yearfatigueliferequirementsofDNVNotationsPlus-2andCSA-2, basedonthedynamicloadingofaNorthAtlanticwavenvironment.
Specialconsiderationhasbeengiventoitemsuchasanti-icing, de-icing, lifesavingequipment, workingareas, navigationsystems, deckmachineryandlivingquarters, withregardtothecoldoperatingconditions. Inaddition, DNVCOMF-V(1) requirementsforvibrationandnoiselevelsintheaccommodationarecompliedwith, alongwithCOMF-C(2), relatingtoairconditioningatverylowambientemperatures. Extended, coveredbridgewingsareanotherconcessiontotheproblemsofharshweather.
ThevesselispoweredbyaKawasakiUA-400turbine, suppliedwithsteamfromtwodual-fuel (HFO/boil-offgas) watertubeboilersandeveloping27,00kW. Adouble-reduction, tandem-articulated, reductiongearboxisfittedinthedrivetoanFPpropeller. Twosteamturbine-driven3250kWalternatorsandadiesel-poweredsetofsimilaroutputareinstalledtosatisfyelectricloadings. Double-hullfueltanksandahigh-performanceoily-waterseparatorareamongstenvironmentalfeaturesadopted. Cargohandlingisbymeansofeight (twoforeachtank) electricsubmergedpumps, eachof1350m3/hduty. Loadingisaccomplishedbyshorepumps.
Awavemonitoringsystemisfitted, andsensorsarepositionedatmajorhullstructurepartstomeasurestresslevelscausedbywavesduringnavigation, whilstmanoeuvrabilityisenhancedbyahigh-liftSchillingrudderandabowthruster. Alsoinstalledisanautomatedballastexchangesystem.

Totalnumberofsistershipstillonorder: ..........................................2 BERGENANTONGisafullyrefrigeratedLPG/NH3tankerbuiltowhathasdevelopedintoasomewhatstandardlayoutforthistypeofvessel, featuringasingle-skin, flushdeckedhullwithoutforecastle, butwiththeupperdeckgivenaslightsheerforward, inlieu. Themooringdeckaftisunkenandtheflatprofileisrelievedonlybythefive-tiersuperstructureaft, housingtheaccommodation.
Thecargospace, stretchingforwardfromthedeckhouse, isdividedintofourholdseachavingtopandbottomwingballastanks, andcontaininganindependent, free-standing, saddle-supportedprismaticargotankmanufacturedfromlow-temperaturecarbonsteel. Designedforcarryingcargoesataminimumof -50ºCandamaximumvapourpressureof0.25bar, thetanksareinsulatedwith120mm-thickpolyurethanefoamcladwith0.5mmaluminium/zincsteelsheet.
Cargoesoftype2Gcanbeloaded, includinganhydrousammonia, 1,3-butadiene, butane (bothISOandnormal), butylenes, commercialpropane, andpropylene, togetherwithotherproductswhosetoxicity, aggressiveness, pressure, temperature, andspecificgravityarewithinthelimitsofthedesign. CargoishandledbymeansoftwoHamworthy-Svanehøjdeepwellpumpsineachtank (eightintotal), eachavingacapacityof600m3/handcapableofprovidingadischargetimeofapproximately18hours, excludingstripping. Loadingisalsoaccomplishedinabout18hours, basedonvapoureturntoshore.
ThengineeringaffiliateofHyundaiHeavyIndustriesbuiltheMANB&W6S60MC-CmainengineinstalledinBergeNantong. Thisdevelops13,560kWMCRat105rev/min, enablingthevesseltosailataservicespeedof16.75knotsatanNCRof12,044kW (89% MCR). ThesamecompanyalsomanufacturedunderlicencethethreeMANB&W5L28/32Hprimemoversforthealternatorsets (producedbyHyundai'selectricaldivision), whicheachsupply100kWtosatisfyelectricalrequirements.

Totalnumberofsistershipstillonorder:.........2 ( (plus 2 small version) ) THEsignificanceofthisnew, five-shipclassofNorwegiancoastalferryliesnotsomuchwiththevesseldesign, butwiththechoiceofpropellingmachineryanditsoperation. BuiltoprovidethenecessarywaterbornelinksonthemajorE39roadbetweenBergenandStavanger, wheretheywillreplacexistingvesselsoperatingbetweenHalhjem/Sandvikvåg, andAarsvågen/Mortavika, thebasicdesignfollowsthatofthemanydouble-endedferriesworkingontheNorwegiancoast. Thus, theyhaveahullgivenovertovehicleaccommodationandaccessedfromeitherend, surmountedbyacentralsuperstructuretoppedwithanavigatingbridge, fromwhichthevesselcanbeconnedintherequiredsailingdirection, thusobviatingtime- consumingturningmanoeuvres.
TwoversionsofthisLMGMarindesignarebeingbuilt.
Ineachcasethehulls, whichareofthesamedimensions, arebeingconstructedatheAkerTulceashipyardinRomania, followingwhichtheyaretowedtotheAkerBrattvåg (Søviknes) siteinNorwayforfittingout.
Bergensfjordisthefirstunitofalargervehiclecapacity, andslightlyfaster, three-shipgroupcarrying212privatecars/22trailersontwodecks, withtheothertwovesselsloading145carsonasingledeck. Vehicleaccessisbywayofdoors/rampsandvisorsateachend, andpassengersenterthroughsidedoorsinthesuperstructure, withinwhichlounge-typeseatingisprovidedfor587persons.
Sevendouble- andfoursingle-berthcabinsareavailableforcrew.
Theinnovativemachineryinstallationadoptedforbothalternativesofthisnewdesigniscentredupontheuseofliquidnaturalgasasthemainfuelforthepropulsionplant.
CleanLNGisreadilyavailablefromNorway'sNorthSeaoilfields, andacoastalsupplyandistributionetworkforbunkeringiscurrentlybeingestablished, sincethisfuel'suseasareplacementformarinedieselformsamajorpartofthegovernment'splansforestrictionof 'greenhouse' gasemissions. Thisparticularlyfollowsclaimsthat40% ofthecountry'sNOxdischargescomefromitsfishingboat, ferryandothercoastalshippingsources.
TheBergenDieseldivisionofRolls-Roycehasaccumulatedexperienceofbuildingland-based, gas- poweredenginesdatingbackovermanyears, andhastwoprovendesignscurrentlyavailable: theB35:40Vdeveloping440kW/cylinder, andthesmallerK-G4modelof22kWcylinderoutput. ThislatterengineisthetypeselectedfortheBergensfjordseries, andisthefirstmarineversiontobeproduced.
Thedesignfollowsthatofland-basedmachinesbyadoptingtheOtto-cyclelean-burncombustionsystem, claimedtohaveadvantagesoverdual-fuelproposalsofferedbysomeothermanufacturers, whichareunderstoodtohaveproblemsuchasmis-firingandifficultoperationatlowloads. Inaddition, theRolls- Roycedesignisaidtohavespeedyaccelerationandafast- stopabilitywhichwillbeadvantageouswhenapproachingterminalsatrelativelyhighspeed.
Bergensfjord'smachineryinstallationcomprisesagas- electricsystembasedontwoAvanKaickmainalternators, thelargerofwhichdevelops3530kWandisdrivenbyaRolls-RoyceKVGS-16G4engine, withthesecond, smaller, 2650kWsetconnectedtoaKVGS-12G4primemover. PowergeneratedfromthesemachinesisdirectedtothedrivemotorsofthefourazimuthingpropulsionunitsuppliedbySchottel, along-establishedexpertinthisfield.
Thesepropulsorsarepositionedateach 'corner' ofthehull, andareoftherecentlyintroducedSchottelCombiDrive (SCD) design. Thiscombinestheattributesofthenewerpodriveswiththoseofthearlier, highlysuccessfulmechanicalRudderpropellermodels (butwiththelectricdrivemotorfittedverticallyinthesupportubeoftheunitinsteadofwithinthepod).
BergensfjordanditstwosistersareachfittedwithSCD2020, twin-propellerversionsoftheSchottelunits, withapropellerateachendofthepodandacapabilityforazimuthingthrough360deg. Eachasaratingof2750kW, whichallowsthesethreevesselstoperatetheHalhjem- to-Sandvikvågservicearoundtheclockat21knots. Thetwosmallervesselsintheseriesemploylesspowerful1600kWSchottelpropulsionunitsofthedifferentSTP1515typetogiveaslower, 17knotperformanceontheAarsvågen-Mortavikaroute.

Totalnumberofsistershipstillonorder: ..........................................1 IllustrationshowscomputerimpressiononlyNORWEGIANnavalarchitecturalconsultancySkipskonsulent, nowoperatingaspartofthequallywell-knownVik-Sandvikconsultancygroup, iscurrentlyexpandingitstanker-designportfolio, andsomexamplesofthevaryingrangeofshipsofthistypefeaturedtherecanbefoundelsewhereinthisreview. ThecompanyismuchinvolvedwiththeChineseshipbuildingindustry, andathepresentimehasvesselsunderconstructiontoitsdesignsintheQingshanandJinlingyards, aswellaswithShanghaiEdward, builderofBitOklandandasistertobecompletedearlynextyear.
ThesevesselsarexamplesofSkipskonsulent'sSK4326, 25,00dwtIMOTypeIIchemical/productankers, andasuchtheyexhibitheirdesigner'semphasisonsafetybyfeaturingatwin-skeghullwithredundancyintheformoftwinmedium-speedengines, twoCPpropellers, andtwinrotary-vanesteeringearscontrollingtworudderswhich, togetherwithapowerfulbowthrusterof1450kWoutput, expressthemanoeuvringabilitiesofthedesign, andcontributetoafacilityformakingquickturn-aroundsinport - afeaturefurtherenhancedbytheinclusionofa 'superstripping' cargohandlingsystemforemptyingtanksquickly.
BitOklandisadouble-hulltankerwitheightpairsofcargotanksofvaryingsizestosuitparcelcargoes. Apoopandforecastleareprovided, linkedbyatrunkontheupperdeck, whichispositionedonthecentreline.
Thetankdivisionsareformedbyacorrugatedcentrelineandtransversebulkheads, and, withdeckstiffeningexternal, andsideframingwithinthedoublehullspace, aplainsurfaceisprovidedsuitableforaphenolicepoxycoating. Twosloptanksarebuiltintotheforendofthepoop, andaninterestingshelterisarrangedontheforecastleprotectingthemooringposition. AlthoughAmarantawasfittedwithaSulzermainengine, othershipsofthat8234designarepoweredbyaMANB&W8K98MC-Cunit; however, thishasbeenchangedforCharlotteWulff, whichasaseven-cylinder, Mk6versionoftheK98MC-seriesengine. The7K98MCenginedevelops40,040kWat94rev/minandproducesafastservicespeedof24.5knotsat90% MCR, onlymarginallylessthanAmaranta.

Becauseoftheincreaseinreefer-boxintake, thelectricaloadingofthe8276designhasbeenincreased, andfivealternatorshavebeeninstalledtomeethedemand. AllareofMANB&W/Dozamelmanufacture, withthreehavinganoutputof1890kW, andtwo1680kW.

Twoflap-typeruddersarefitted, withmanoeuvrabilityenhancedbytwo200kWCPbowthrusters. Formooringpurposes, twoself-tensioning, electricallydriven, combinedanchorwindlass/winchesarefittedontheforecastle, andfourself-tensioningwinchesaft.

Totalnumberofsistershipstillonorder:..................................................Nil PERHAPSoneofthemostsignificantshipsdeliveredfromTurkeythisyearisFSCharlotte, an11,00dwtcombinedmoltensulphurandbitumentanker. DesignedbyDeltaMarine, ofIstanbul, thisinterestingvesselwashandedovertoherowner, FouquetSacopMaritime, ofFrance, inMarch2006, bytheYardimciShipyardgroup. Sheisoneofonlyveryfewvesselsofthistypeinserviceworldwideandisnowonlong-termchartertoTotal.
FSCharlotteisasingle-decked, single-screwtanker, withadoublebottomandoubleskin, andhasatotalof11cargotanksandtwosloptanks. Sixofthecargotanksaredesignedtocarrymoltensulphur (1.80tonne/m3) at180ºCandfivetocarrybitumen (1.30tonne/m3) at250ºC. Thecargotanksarefullyindependentofthehullstructure, andmountedonspecialsupports, toallowforexpansionofthecargoathightemperatures; thus, FSCharlotteis, effectively, atriple-hullship.
Eachofthecargotanks, whichcanexpandupto80mm, weighsaround400tonnes, andthispresentedasignificantchallengetothedesigner. TheUlepsitanksupportsystemfromtheDutchcompanyBeeleEngineeringwaselectedforthevessel; thisystemwasabletodemonstratethatitcouldmeetveryspecificrequirements, afterextensivestrength, thermalandCFDanalyseswerecarriedoutbyMeshEngineeringCo.
ThecargodischargesystemisbasedaroundfourBornemannhydraulicpumpsintwoseparaterooms.
Twopumpseachaveacapacityof400m3/h, forbitumen, andtwoareratedat337m3/hformoltensulphur.
Considerableattentionalsohadtobepaidtotheffectivenessofthetankinsulationsystem, sothatintheventofanytechnicalproblems, thecargotemperaturecanbemaintainedsufficientlytokeepthecargoesliquid, sothatheycanstillbepumpedashore.
Thedailycargoheatloss, intheventofafailureoftheheatingsystem, iscalculatedtobeonly1ºC.
ThehullformofFSCharlottehasbeendesignedtominimiseresistancetobothfrictionandwaves.
ResistanceandpoweringtestswerecarriedoutinIstanbulTechnicalUniversity'sAtaNutkuShipModelTestingLaboratory. DeltaMarineclaimsthatheoveralldesignprovidesanenvironment-friendly, cost-effective, reliable, andflexibleunit.
Thetanker'sclassificationcoversanextensivelistofrequirementsfromBureauVeritas, includingthoseforvibrationandnoise, andthestructurehasadditionallybeenanalysedtocomplywiththeBVeristarnotation.
ThepropulsionplantconsistsofanMaKmainengine, havinganoutputpowerof5400kWat500rev/min. Thetransmissionistakenthroughareductiongearbox (fittedwithapowertake-offshaftforanalternator) toaCPpropellerof4400mmdiameter, turningat150rev/min. Three750kWheavy- fuel-burningdieselgeneratorsareinstalled, andheatforallcargoandomesticservicesisgeneratedbytwothermaloilboilersandaneconomiser.
Toincreasemanoeuvringcapabilities, an800kWbowthrusterisfitted, andtherearefoursetsoftwo-drumooringwinches, includingtwosetswithwindlasses.
Accommodationisarrangedfor19people, plusahospitalandapilot/owner'scabin, allwithseparatetoiletandshower.

Totalnumberofsistershipstillonorder: ..........................................3 THESevernavshipyardislocatedatDrobetaTurnuSeverin, ontheriverDanubeinwesternRomania, neartheYugoslavborder. Althoughbetterknownasabuilderofspecialistriver/canalcargovesselsoperatingonRussianandEasternEuropeanwaterways, thisyardhasfeaturedsea-goingvessels, includingtankers, initsportfolio; nevertheless, GaschemShinano, consideredtobeoneofthemostsophisticatedethylenetankersnowinservice, givestheyard'soperationsanimportantnewthrust.
Thedesign, includingasplantlayoutandengineering, waspreparedbyGermanconsultantHBHunteEngineeringinco-operationwiththeowner, andfeaturesasingle-deck, engine-afthullwithtwocargoholds. Theaftoneisingle-skinnedwithupperwingvoidspaces, andcontainsabi-lobecargotank, whilstheforwardcompartmentismadebox-shapedbyadoubleskinformingvoidsandballastanks, andhasasinglecylindricaltankinstalled.
Bothtanksareconstructedof5% nickelsteeltoadesignpressureof5.5bar(g), andtheplantisuitablefortransportingmostsemi-refrigeratedcargoesintheIMOGasCode, withinatemperaturerangeof -104oC/+35oC, andSGbelow0.972. Whencarryingchemicals, spoolpiecesarefittedinthepipingsystemtodisconnecthereliquefactionplant, andthesearealsousedwhentwodifferentcargoesaretransportedandcooledathesametime.
Thecargotanksarenotcoatedinternallybutareinsulatedexternallywitha170mmCryopurfoamapplication. Deepwellpumpsof200m3/hdutyareinstalledinsumpsatheaftendofthetankstohandlecargo, witha300m3/hboosterpumpositionedamidships, nearthemanifold, toassistwithlongjettypipelines. Gasdomesfittedtothefrontofthetankscontainallpipeconnections, withcargoperationscontrolledbyhydraulicallyactuatedvalveseitherlocallyorfromthecargocontroloffice.
Thereliquefactionplantishousedinanopenshelterondeck. ThishasavapourareacontainingBurckhardt (formerlySulzer) compressors, suctionseparatorsandeconomisers, andaliquidareafittedwithmulti-purposeheatexchangers (MPHE) andmodularefrigerantunits; thelatterincorporatethecargocondensersandMycondouble-screwcompressors. TheMPHEvariouslyserveasgascooler, condenser, gaseparator, gasheater (usingseawaterasaheatingmedium) andvaporiserforpurgingtanksbeforeuse. Thecompletegas-handlingplantwasdesignedandsuppliedjointlybytheownerandHBHunteEngineering.
Anitrogenplantisinstalledintheforecastleandoperatesonthepressure-swingsystem, supplying99.9% puregasforpaddingandpurgingpurposes, aswellasprovidingdryairofdewpoint -55oC. Thegasplantistartedlocallybutisremotelycontrolledbycomputerised, redundantunitswithmonitorsandalarmsinimportantlocations.
ThemainengineisofMaK9M32Cdesign, developing4500kWat600rev/minandrivingaCPpropellerthroughaRenkgearboxforaservicespeedof16knotsathe 'ethylene' draught, and17knotsinballast.
A1500kWshaft-drivenalternatorisfitted, capablealoneofservingtheneedsofthereliquefactionplant, andtherearealsotwodiesel-drivenalternatorsof1138kVAoutputavailable. Bothmainandauxiliaryenginesarefresh-water-cooledusingplatecoolers, andathermaloilplantservedfromexhaust-gasandauxiliaryboilersmaintainsthebunkerfueltemperature.
ABarkeflaprudderanda400kWbowthrusterarefittedtoenhancemanoeuvrability.

Totalnumberofsistershipstillonorder: ..........................................3 SUCCESIVEexamplesofLindenau's 'SafetyTanker' serieshavefeaturedineditionsofSignificantShipseversinceitsintroductionin1990. Whilsthecharacteristicsofthedesignshaveremainedthesame, almosteveryvariantofthefirst23,400dwtvesselhasdemonstratedsomevolutionarysolutiontoenvironmentalconditions. Seatroutisthefirstofthe 'SafetyClass2010' type, thelatestinthisprogressionofdesignsandisofferedwith40,600dwt.
Itfollowsthebasiconfigurationoftheconceptbyhavingadoublehullsurroundingnotonlyanarrangementofivepairsofcargoandthreesloptanks, butofthefueltanksinthengineroom. Thetankdivisionsareformedfromvolume (double-skin) transverseandlongitudinalbulkheadsofferingasmoothtanksurfaceprotectedbyanEpiconT800coating.
Allcargopipes, fittings, valves, togetherwiththe10Svanehøj600m3/hsubmergedcargopumps, andtheheatingcoilsprovidedintanks6and7, aremadeofstainlessteel. Gaininganextra300dwthasmeantanincreaseindimensionsfortheSeatroutclassoverearlier 'SafetyTanker' designs, andbeamhasnowreachedPanamaxsize. IthasalsobeenecessarytoaddtwocylinderstotheMANB&WL58/64typemainenginewhichasbeenusedinallpreviousvariants, inordertoachieveacomparableshipspeed; theincreased11,200kWoutputfromthe8L58/64unitdrivesthroughaRenkgearboxandVulkancoupling, meetingacontractspeedof16.50knots (15.50knotsonseatrialsat8200kW).
Tomaintainperformanceinaneconomicandenvironmentalfriendlyway, LindenauhasemployedextensiveCFD (computationalfluidynamics) studiesonthehullform, andpaidparticularattentiontothefore-endlineswithregardtostructuralstresses, lossofspeedinaseaway, fueleconomy, andeckwetness.
Operationsathighspeedinice, andgoodicebreakingcapabilities, havealsobeenaddressed.
IthasalwaysbeenclaimedthatheLindenaudesignsarequalto, ifnotaheadofmostcurrentclassificationandenviromentalrequirements, thusfeaturesuchasfixedgasdetection, compliancewith 'GreenPassport' recommendations, waterballastmanagement, reductionofNOxandSOxemissions, vapoureturn, sewagetreatment, choiceofcoolantsandfirefightingagents, alsominimalbilgeandoilresidues, arenowstandard.
Cargoheatingemploysindividual, deck-mountedheatexchangersforeachtank, andanotableinclusionisafixedemergencydischargesystemwhichallowsunloadingofcargotocontinueintheventofpumpfailure. Allaspectsofcargocontrolarecomputerisedandmachineryoperationsarehandledbyanintegratedcontrolandpowermanagementsystem. Anemergencytowingfacilityisalsofittedatbowandstern.
